\nopandoc{\begin{otherlanguage}{english}}

## The Song of Moses
# 32
\bibleverse{1} Give ear, you heavens, and I will speak. Let the earth hear the words of my mouth. \bibleverse{2} My doctrine will drop as the rain. My speech will condense as the dew, as the misty rain on the tender grass, as the showers on the herb. \bibleverse{3} For I will proclaim Yahweh’s name. Ascribe greatness to our God! \bibleverse{4} The Rock: his work is perfect, for all his ways are just. A God of faithfulness who does no wrong, just and right is he. \bibleverse{5} They have dealt corruptly with him. They are not his children, because of their defect. They are a perverse and crooked generation. \bibleverse{6} Is this the way you repay Yahweh, foolish and unwise people? Isn’t he your father who has bought you? He has made you and established you. \bibleverse{7} Remember the days of old. Consider the years of many generations. Ask your father, and he will show you; your elders, and they will tell you. \bibleverse{8} When the Most High gave to the nations their inheritance, when he separated the children of men, he set the bounds of the peoples according to the number of the children of Israel. \bibleverse{9} For Yahweh’s portion is his people. Jacob is the lot of his inheritance. \bibleverse{10} He found him in a desert land, in the waste howling wilderness. He surrounded him. He cared for him. He kept him as the apple of his eye. \bibleverse{11} As an eagle that stirs up her nest, that flutters over her young, he spread abroad his wings, he took them, he bore them on his feathers. \bibleverse{12} Yahweh alone led him. There was no foreign god with him. \bibleverse{13} He made him ride on the high places of the earth. He ate the increase of the field. He caused him to suck honey out of the rock, oil out of the flinty rock; \bibleverse{14} butter from the herd, and milk from the flock, with fat of lambs, rams of the breed of Bashan, and goats, with the finest of the wheat. From the blood of the grape, you drank wine. \bibleverse{15} But Jeshurun grew fat, and kicked. You have grown fat. You have grown thick. You have become sleek. Then he abandoned God who made him, and rejected the Rock of his salvation. \bibleverse{16} They moved him to jealousy with strange gods. They provoked him to anger with abominations. \bibleverse{17} They sacrificed to demons, not God, to gods that they didn’t know, to new gods that came up recently, which your fathers didn’t dread. \bibleverse{18} Of the Rock who became your father, you are unmindful, and have forgotten God who gave you birth. \bibleverse{19} Yahweh saw and abhorred, because of the provocation of his sons and his daughters. \bibleverse{20} He said, “I will hide my face from them. I will see what their end will be; for they are a very perverse generation, children in whom is no faithfulness. \bibleverse{21} They have moved me to jealousy with that which is not God. They have provoked me to anger with their vanities. I will move them to jealousy with those who are not a people. I will provoke them to anger with a foolish nation. \bibleverse{22} For a fire is kindled in my anger, that burns to the lowest Sheol,^[**32:22** Sheol is the place of the dead.] devours the earth with its increase, and sets the foundations of the mountains on fire. \bibleverse{23} “I will heap evils on them. I will spend my arrows on them. \bibleverse{24} They shall be wasted with hunger, and devoured with burning heat and bitter destruction. I will send the teeth of animals on them, with the venom of vipers that glide in the dust. \bibleverse{25} Outside the sword will bereave, and in the rooms, terror on both young man and virgin, the nursing infant with the gray-haired man. \bibleverse{26} I said that I would scatter them afar. I would make their memory to cease from among men; \bibleverse{27} were it not that I feared the provocation of the enemy, lest their adversaries should judge wrongly, lest they should say, ‘Our hand is exalted; Yahweh has not done all this.’” \bibleverse{28} For they are a nation void of counsel. There is no understanding in them. \bibleverse{29} Oh that they were wise, that they understood this, that they would consider their latter end! \bibleverse{30} How could one chase a thousand, and two put ten thousand to flight, unless their Rock had sold them, and Yahweh had delivered them up? \bibleverse{31} For their rock is not as our Rock, even our enemies themselves concede. \bibleverse{32} For their vine is of the vine of Sodom, of the fields of Gomorrah. Their grapes are poison grapes. Their clusters are bitter. \bibleverse{33} Their wine is the poison of serpents, the cruel venom of asps. \bibleverse{34} “Isn’t this laid up in store with me, sealed up among my treasures? \bibleverse{35} Vengeance is mine, and recompense, at the time when their foot slides, for the day of their calamity is at hand. Their doom rushes at them.” \bibleverse{36} For Yahweh will judge his people, and have compassion on his servants, when he sees that their power is gone, that there is no one remaining, shut up or left at large. \bibleverse{37} He will say, “Where are their gods, the rock in which they took refuge, \bibleverse{38} which ate the fat of their sacrifices, and drank the wine of their drink offering? Let them rise up and help you! Let them be your protection. \bibleverse{39} “See now that I myself am he. There is no god with me. I kill and I make alive. I wound and I heal. There is no one who can deliver out of my hand. \bibleverse{40} For I lift up my hand to heaven and declare, as I live forever, \bibleverse{41} if I sharpen my glittering sword, my hand grasps it in judgment; I will take vengeance on my adversaries, and will repay those who hate me. \bibleverse{42} I will make my arrows drunk with blood. My sword shall devour flesh with the blood of the slain and the captives, from the head of the leaders of the enemy.” \bibleverse{43} Rejoice, you nations, with his people, for he will avenge the blood of his servants. He will take vengeance on his adversaries, and will make atonement for his land and for his people.^[**32:43** For this verse, LXX reads: Rejoice, you heavens, with him, and let all the angels of God worship him; rejoice you Gentiles, with his people, and let all the sons of God strengthen themselves in him; for he will avenge the blood of his sons, and he will render vengeance, and recompense justice to his enemies, and will reward them that hate him; and the Lord shall purge the land of his people.]

## Last promulgation of the law; Moses receives instructions about his impending death
\bibleverse{44} Moses came and spoke all the words of this song in the ears of the people, he and Joshua the son of Nun. \bibleverse{45} Moses finished reciting all these words to all Israel. \bibleverse{46} He said to them, “Set your heart to all the words which I testify to you today, which you shall command your children to observe to do, all the words of this law. \bibleverse{47} For it is no vain thing for you, because it is your life, and through this thing you shall prolong your days in the land, where you go over the Jordan to possess it.” \bibleverse{48} Yahweh spoke to Moses that same day, saying, \bibleverse{49} “Go up into this mountain of Abarim, to Mount Nebo, which is in the land of Moab, that is across from Jericho; and see the land of Canaan, which I give to the children of Israel for a possession. \bibleverse{50} Die on the mountain where you go up, and be gathered to your people, as Aaron your brother died on Mount Hor, and was gathered to his people; \bibleverse{51} because you trespassed against me among the children of Israel at the waters of Meribah of Kadesh, in the wilderness of Zin; because you didn’t uphold my holiness among the children of Israel. \bibleverse{52} For you shall see the land from a distance; but you shall not go there into the land which I give the children of Israel.” 

\nopandoc{\end{otherlanguage}}
\switchcolumn[0]*

## La bendición de despedida de Moisés sobre las doce tribus de Israel
# 33
\bibleverse{1} Esta es la bendición con la que Moisés, el hombre de Dios, bendijo a los hijos de Israel antes de su muerte. ^[**33:1** Gén 49,1] \bibleverse{2} Dijo, “Yahvé vino desde el Sinaí, y se levantó de Seir hacia ellos. Brilló desde el monte Parán. Él vino de los diez mil santos. A su derecha había una ley de fuego para ellos. ^[**33:2** otro manuscrito dice “Vino con miríadas de santos del sur, de las laderas de sus montañas”.] ^[**33:2** Jds 1,14] \bibleverse{3} Sí, ama al pueblo. Todos sus santos están en tu mano. Se sentaron a sus pies. Cada uno recibe sus palabras. \bibleverse{4} Moisés nos ordenó una ley, una herencia para la asamblea de Jacob. \bibleverse{5} Fue rey en Jeshurun, cuando los jefes del pueblo estaban reunidos, todas las tribus de Israel juntas. ^[**33:5** Éxod 15,18; Is 44,2; Éxod 19,7-8]

## Bendiciones para las tribus individuales
\bibleverse{6} “Que Rubén viva y no muera; Ni que sus hombres sean pocos”.

\bibleverse{7} Esto es para Judá. Él dijo, “Escucha, Yahvé, la voz de Judá. Llévalo a su pueblo. Con sus manos contendió por sí mismo. Serás una ayuda contra sus adversarios”.

\bibleverse{8} Sobre Leví dijo, “Tu Thummim y tu Urim están con tu divino, que probó en Massah, con el que te enfrentaste en las aguas de Meribah. ^[**33:8** Éxod 28,30; Éxod 17,1-17; Núm 20,1] \bibleverse{9} Dijo de su padre y de su madre: “No lo he visto”. No reconoció a sus hermanos, ni conocía a sus propios hijos; porque han observado tu palabra, y mantener tu pacto. ^[**33:9** Mat 10,37; Éxod 32,26-29] \bibleverse{10} Ellos enseñarán a Jacob tus ordenanzas, e Israel su ley. Pondrán incienso ante ti, y el holocausto completo en tu altar. \bibleverse{11} Yahvé, bendice sus habilidades. Acepta el trabajo de sus manos. Golpea las caderas de los que se levantan contra él, de los que le odian, para que no vuelvan a levantarse”.

\bibleverse{12} Sobre Benjamín dijo, “El amado de Yahvé habitará en seguridad junto a él. Lo cubre todo el día. Habita entre sus hombros”.

\bibleverse{13} Sobre José dijo, “Su tierra está bendecida por Yahvé, por las cosas preciosas de los cielos, por el rocío, por lo profundo que se encuentra debajo, \bibleverse{14} por las cosas preciosas de los frutos del sol, por las cosas preciosas que puede dar la luna, \bibleverse{15} para las mejores cosas de las antiguas montañas, por las cosas preciosas de las colinas eternas, \bibleverse{16} por las cosas preciosas de la tierra y su plenitud, la buena voluntad del que vivía en el monte. ^[**33:16** decir, la zarza ardiente de Éxodo 3:3-4.] Que esto venga en la cabeza de José, en la corona de la cabeza del que fue separado de sus hermanos. ^[**33:16** Éxod 3,2; Gén 49,26] \bibleverse{17} La majestad pertenece al primogénito de su rebaño. Sus cuernos son los cuernos del buey salvaje. Con ellos empujará a todos los pueblos hasta los confines de la tierra. Son los diez mil de Efraín. Son los miles de Manasés”.

\bibleverse{18} Sobre Zebulón dijo, “Alégrate, Zabulón, en tu salida; e Isacar, en sus tiendas. \bibleverse{19} Llamarán a los pueblos a la montaña. Allí ofrecerán sacrificios de justicia, porque sacarán la abundancia de los mares, los tesoros ocultos de la arena”.

\bibleverse{20} Sobre Gad dijo, “El que agranda a Gad es bendecido. Habita como una leona, y desgarra el brazo y la coronilla. \bibleverse{21} La primera parte la proporcionó él mismo, porque la porción del legislador estaba reservada para él. Vino con los jefes del pueblo. Ejecutó la justicia de Yahvé, Sus ordenanzas con Israel”. ^[**33:21** Núm 32,1]

\bibleverse{22} Sobre Dan dijo, “Dan es un cachorro de leónque salta de Basán”.

\bibleverse{23} Sobre Neftalí dijo, “Neftalí, satisfecho con el favor, llena de la bendición de Yahvé, Poseer el oeste y el sur”.

\bibleverse{24} Sobre Asher dijo, “Asher ha sido bendecido con hijos. Que sea aceptable para sus hermanos. Que moje el pie en aceite. \bibleverse{25} Sus barras serán de hierro y bronce. Como tus días, así será tu fuerza.

## Alabado sea el Señor y bendito Israel
\bibleverse{26} “No hay nadie como Dios, Jeshurun, que cabalga por los cielos en busca de su ayuda, en su excelencia en los cielos. ^[**33:26** Is 44,2] \bibleverse{27} El Dios eterno es tu morada. Debajo están los brazos eternos. Expulsó al enemigo de delante de ti, y dijo: “¡Destruye! \bibleverse{28} Israel vive en seguridad, la fuente de Jacob solo, En una tierra de grano y vino nuevo. Sí, sus cielos dejan caer el rocío. ^[**33:28** Núm 23,9] \bibleverse{29} ¡Eres feliz, Israel! Que es como tú, un pueblo salvado por Yahvé, el escudo de su ayuda, ¿la espada de su excelencia? Tus enemigos se someterán a ti. Pisarás sus lugares altos”. ^[**33:29** Deut 4,7-8; Sal 33,12; Sal 144,15]

\switchcolumn
\nopandoc{\begin{otherlanguage}{english}}

## Moses' Farewell Blessing on the Twelve Tribes of Israel
# 33
\bibleverse{1} This is the blessing with which Moses the man of God blessed the children of Israel before his death. \bibleverse{2} He said, “Yahweh came from Sinai, and rose from Seir to them. He shone from Mount Paran. He came from the ten thousands of holy ones. At his right hand was a fiery law for them.^[**33:2** another manuscript reads “He came with myriads of holy ones from the south, from his mountain slopes.”] \bibleverse{3} Yes, he loves the people. All his saints are in your hand. They sat down at your feet. Each receives your words. \bibleverse{4} Moses commanded us a law, an inheritance for the assembly of Jacob. \bibleverse{5} He was king in Jeshurun, when the heads of the people were gathered, all the tribes of Israel together.

## Blessings to the individual tribes
\bibleverse{6} “Let Reuben live, and not die; Nor let his men be few.” \bibleverse{7} This is for Judah. He said, “Hear, Yahweh, the voice of Judah. Bring him in to his people. With his hands he contended for himself. You shall be a help against his adversaries.” \bibleverse{8} About Levi he said, “Your Thummim and your Urim are with your godly one, whom you proved at Massah, with whom you contended at the waters of Meribah. \bibleverse{9} He said of his father, and of his mother, ‘I have not seen him.’ He didn’t acknowledge his brothers, nor did he know his own children; for they have observed your word, and keep your covenant. \bibleverse{10} They shall teach Jacob your ordinances, and Israel your law. They shall put incense before you, and whole burnt offering on your altar. \bibleverse{11} Yahweh, bless his skills. Accept the work of his hands. Strike through the hips of those who rise up against him, of those who hate him, that they not rise again.” \bibleverse{12} About Benjamin he said, “The beloved of Yahweh will dwell in safety by him. He covers him all day long. He dwells between his shoulders.” \bibleverse{13} About Joseph he said, “His land is blessed by Yahweh, for the precious things of the heavens, for the dew, for the deep that couches beneath, \bibleverse{14} for the precious things of the fruits of the sun, for the precious things that the moon can yield, \bibleverse{15} for the best things of the ancient mountains, for the precious things of the everlasting hills, \bibleverse{16} for the precious things of the earth and its fullness, the good will of him who lived in the bush.^[**33:16** i. e., the burning bush of Exodus 3:3-4.] Let this come on the head of Joseph, on the crown of the head of him who was separated from his brothers. \bibleverse{17} Majesty belongs to the firstborn of his herd. His horns are the horns of the wild ox. With them he will push all the peoples to the ends of the earth. They are the ten thousands of Ephraim. They are the thousands of Manasseh.” \bibleverse{18} About Zebulun he said, “Rejoice, Zebulun, in your going out; and Issachar, in your tents. \bibleverse{19} They will call the peoples to the mountain. There they will offer sacrifices of righteousness, for they will draw out the abundance of the seas, the hidden treasures of the sand.” \bibleverse{20} About Gad he said, “He who enlarges Gad is blessed. He dwells as a lioness, and tears the arm and the crown of the head. \bibleverse{21} He provided the first part for himself, for the lawgiver’s portion was reserved for him. He came with the heads of the people. He executed the righteousness of Yahweh, His ordinances with Israel.” \bibleverse{22} About Dan he said, “Dan is a lion’s cub that leaps out of Bashan.” \bibleverse{23} About Naphtali he said, “Naphtali, satisfied with favor, full of Yahweh’s blessing, Possess the west and the south.” \bibleverse{24} About Asher he said, “Asher is blessed with children. Let him be acceptable to his brothers. Let him dip his foot in oil. \bibleverse{25} Your bars will be iron and bronze. As your days, so your strength will be.

## Praise the Lord and blessed Israel
\bibleverse{26} “There is no one like God, Jeshurun, who rides on the heavens for your help, in his excellency on the skies. \bibleverse{27} The eternal God is your dwelling place. Underneath are the everlasting arms. He thrust out the enemy from before you, and said, ‘Destroy!’ \bibleverse{28} Israel dwells in safety, the fountain of Jacob alone, In a land of grain and new wine. Yes, his heavens drop down dew. \bibleverse{29} You are happy, Israel! Who is like you, a people saved by Yahweh, the shield of your help, the sword of your excellency? Your enemies will submit themselves to you. You will tread on their high places.” 

\nopandoc{\end{otherlanguage}}
\switchcolumn[0]*

## Moisés en el monte Nebo; su muerte y entierro; Joshua lo sucederá
# 34
\bibleverse{1} Moisés subió desde las llanuras de Moab hasta el monte Nebo, a la cima del Pisga, que está frente a Jericó. Yahvé le mostró toda la tierra de Galaad hasta Dan, ^[**34:1** Deut 3,27] \bibleverse{2} y todo Neftalí, y la tierra de Efraín y Manasés, y toda la tierra de Judá, hasta el Mar Occidental, \bibleverse{3} y el sur,^[**34:3** o, Negev] y la llanura del valle de Jericó la ciudad de las palmeras, hasta Zoar. \bibleverse{4} Yahvé le dijo: “Esta es la tierra que juré a Abraham, a Isaac y a Jacob, diciendo: ‘La daré a tu descendencia’. He hecho que la veas con tus ojos, pero no pasarás por allí”. ^[**34:4** Gén 12,7]

\bibleverse{5} Así murió Moisés, siervo del Señor, en la tierra de Moab, según la palabra del Señor. ^[**34:5** Deut 32,50] \bibleverse{6} Lo enterró en el valle de la tierra de Moab, frente a Bet Peor, pero nadie sabe dónde está su tumba hasta el día de hoy. ^[**34:6** Jds 1,9] \bibleverse{7} Moisés tenía ciento veinte años cuando murió. Su ojo no se oscureció, ni su fuerza se agotó. \bibleverse{8} Los hijos de Israel lloraron a Moisés en las llanuras de Moab durante treinta días, hasta que terminaron los días de llanto por Moisés. ^[**34:8** Núm 20,29] \bibleverse{9} Josué, hijo de Nun, estaba lleno de espíritu de sabiduría, porque Moisés había puesto sus manos sobre él. Los hijos de Israel lo escucharon e hicieron lo que Yahvé le había ordenado a Moisés. ^[**34:9** Núm 27,18]

## Valoración de la grandeza e importancia de Moisés
\bibleverse{10} Desde entonces no ha surgido en Israel un profeta como Moisés, a quien Yahvé conoció cara a cara, ^[**34:10** Éxod 33,11; Núm 12,6-8] \bibleverse{11} en todas las señales y los prodigios que Yahvé le envió a hacer en la tierra de Egipto, al faraón y a todos sus siervos, y a toda su tierra, \bibleverse{12} y en toda la mano poderosa, y en todos los hechos asombrosos, que Moisés hizo a la vista de todo Israel.
\switchcolumn
\nopandoc{\begin{otherlanguage}{english}}

## Moses on Mount Nebo; his death and burial; Joshua will succeed
# 34
\bibleverse{1} Moses went up from the plains of Moab to Mount Nebo, to the top of Pisgah, that is opposite Jericho. Yahweh showed him all the land of Gilead to Dan, \bibleverse{2} and all Naphtali, and the land of Ephraim and Manasseh, and all the land of Judah, to the Western Sea, \bibleverse{3} and the south,^[**34:3** or, Negev] and the Plain of the valley of Jericho the city of palm trees, to Zoar. \bibleverse{4} Yahweh said to him, “This is the land which I swore to Abraham, to Isaac, and to Jacob, saying, ‘I will give it to your offspring.’ I have caused you to see it with your eyes, but you shall not go over there.” \bibleverse{5} So Moses the servant of Yahweh died there in the land of Moab, according to Yahweh’s word. \bibleverse{6} He buried him in the valley in the land of Moab opposite Beth Peor, but no man knows where his tomb is to this day. \bibleverse{7} Moses was one hundred twenty years old when he died. His eye was not dim, nor his strength gone. \bibleverse{8} The children of Israel wept for Moses in the plains of Moab thirty days, until the days of weeping in the mourning for Moses were ended. \bibleverse{9} Joshua the son of Nun was full of the spirit of wisdom, for Moses had laid his hands on him. The children of Israel listened to him, and did as Yahweh commanded Moses.

## Appreciation of the greatness and importance of Moses
\bibleverse{10} Since then, there has not arisen a prophet in Israel like Moses, whom Yahweh knew face to face, \bibleverse{11} in all the signs and the wonders which Yahweh sent him to do in the land of Egypt, to Pharaoh, and to all his servants, and to all his land, \bibleverse{12} and in all the mighty hand, and in all the awesome deeds, which Moses did in the sight of all Israel.
\nopandoc{\end{otherlanguage}}
\nopandoc{\end{paracol}}
